SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CategoryId], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[Image], [t].[Name], [t].[PlayerUrl], [t].[Plot], [t].[Year], [c0].[Id], [c0].[CreatedAt], [c0].[Name], [r].[Id], [r].[CartoonId], [r].[CreatedAt], [r].[UserId], [r].[Value]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [c].[Id], [c].[CategoryId], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[Image], [c].[Name], [c].[PlayerUrl], [c].[Plot], [c].[Year]
    FROM [Cartoons] AS [c]

) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c0] ON [t].[CategoryId] = [c0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Ratings] AS [r] ON [t].[Id] = [r].[CartoonId]
